                # 3. efs license is not present
                ecmd vxdg -g "$_init_dg" adddisk $diskopt
                res=$?
        fi
        if [ $res -ne 0 ]; then
                export _init_dg initdev progname; ewritemsg -s ERROR -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:1327 \
                        "Addition of $initdev to $_init_dg disk group failed." "$@"
                return 10
        fi
}

# remove_swap - remove swap areas on the given disk
#
# If not all swap areas can be removed, then we cannot encapsulate this
# disk.
remove_swap()
{
        
        rmswaplist=`swap -l 2> /dev/null |
                sed -n -e "s%^\(/dev/dsk/\${1}s[0-7]\).*%\1%p" \
                       -e "s%^\(/dev/ap/dsk/\${1}s[0-7]\).*%\1%p"`

        if [ -n "$rmswaplist" ]
        then
                for rmsw in $rmswaplist; do
                        if [ -x /usr/sbin/dumpadm ]
                        then
                                grep $rmsw /etc/dumpadm.conf > /dev/null
                                if [ $? -eq 0 ]
                                then
                                     DUMPADMDIR=/etc/vx/dumpadm.d
                                     mkdir -p $DUMPADMDIR 2>/dev/null
                                     rm -f $DUMPADMDIR/dumpadm.* 2>/dev/null
                                     cp /etc/dumpadm.conf \
                                                 $DUMPADMDIR/dumpadm.conf.orig
                                     dumpadm > $DUMPADMDIR/dumpadm.out.orig
                                     > /etc/vx/.dumpadm
                                else
                                     dumpadm -u 
                                fi
                        fi
                        if ecmd swap -d $rmsw 2> /dev/null
                        then
                                swap_removed="$swap_removed $rmswaplist"
                        else
                                disk=$1; export disk rmsw; ewritemsg -s WARNING -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:108 \
                                 "Cannot delete swap area $rmsw from disk $disk"
                                return 1
                        fi
                done
        fi

        return 0
}

reboot=no; export reboot
first_disk=no
set_OS_variables
swap_removed=

# Remove volumes not needed because of vxunroot

if [ -f $rmvols ]
then
        exec 3<&0 < $rmvols
        while read vol; do
                vxedit -g $RESERVED_DG_BOOT -rf rm $vol
        done
        exec 0<&3 3<&-
        rm -f $rmvols
fi

if [ -f $rmvmdisks ]; then
        exec 3<&0 < $rmvmdisks
        while read disk setup_opts; do
                export disk; ewritemsg -s INFO -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:500 \
                  "Volume Manager: Removing $disk from Volume Manager control."
                dm=`vxdisk -g $RESERVED_DG_BOOT -q list $disk |
                        sed -n 's/disk:.*name=\(.*\) id=.*/\1/p'`

                ### delete any sd of this dm that is preserving priv area
                ### n.b. Can only find sd if sd_putil0 string "PRIVATE" used.
                for nukesd in `vxprint -g $RESERVED_DG_BOOT -q -sn -e "sd_putil0 ~ /PRIVATE/"`; do
                        privdm=`vxprint -g $RESERVED_DG_BOOT -F %disk $nukesd`
                        if [ "$dm" = "$privdm" ]
                        then
                                vxedit -g $RESERVED_DG_BOOT -f rm $nukesd
                        fi
                done

                disk=`vxdisk -g $RESERVED_DG_BOOT list $disk | grep '^Device' | \
                         awk '{print $2}'`
                dogi_slice_to_device $disk disk

                ### OK, now we can get rid of this dm

                ### Figure out if this is the last disk in the disk group

                if [ `vxdisk -qg $RESERVED_DG_BOOT list | wc -l` -eq 1 ]
                then
                        if vxdg destroy $RESERVED_DG_BOOT
                        then
                                vxdctl bootdg $RESERVED_DG_NONE
                        else
                                export dm; ewritemsg -s NOTICE -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:1530 \
"The boot disk group could not be destroyed.  The last disk $dm will be
   marked as reserved so no space from it is accidentally allocated"
                                ecmd vxedit -g $RESERVED_DG_BOOT set reserved=on $dm
                                continue
                        fi
                else
                        if not ecmd vxdg -g $RESERVED_DG_BOOT rmdisk $dm
                        then
                                export dm; ewritemsg -s ERROR -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:1538 \
"The removal of $dm failed. It will be marked as
   reserved so no space from it is accidentally allocated"
                                ecmd vxedit -g $RESERVED_DG_BOOT set reserved=on $dm
                                continue
                        fi
                fi

                ecmd vxdiskunsetup $disk
        done
        exec 0<&3 3<&-
        rm -f $rmvmdisks
fi

[ -f $reconfigfile -a ! -f $mkdbfile ] || exit 0
[ -d $STATEDIR ] || volmkdirs
xcmd cd $STATEDIR

rm -f $reconfigfile
rm -f $pnewerr $pcaperr
sync

if [ -f $pnewfile -o -f $pcapfile ]; then
        ewritemsg -s INFO -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:324 \
                "The Volume Manager is now reconfiguring (partition phase)..."
fi

VXLICTEST=/sbin/vxlictest
licavail=1
if [ -x $VXLICTEST ]
then
        $VXLICTEST -n "VERITAS Volume Manager" -f "VxVM" -sup
        full_lic_avail=$?
        $VXLICTEST -n "VERITAS Volume Manager" -f "VxVM Base" -sup
        base_lic_avail=$?
        $VXLICTEST -n "VERITAS Volume Manager" -f "PHOTON" -sup
        photon_lic_avail=$?
        $VXLICTEST -n "VERITAS Volume Manager" -f "SSA" -sup
        ssa_lic_avail=$?
        if [ $full_lic_avail -eq 0 ] || [ $base_lic_avail -eq 0 ] ||  \
                [ $photon_lic_avail -eq 0 ] || [ $ssa_lic_avail -eq 0 ]
        then
                licavail=0
        fi
fi

if [ -f $pnewfile ]; then
        if [ "$licavail" -eq 1 ]
        then
                ewritemsg -s ERROR -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:873 \
                                "No valid license.  Will not initialize disks"
        fi
        exec 3<&0 < $pnewlist
        while read disk setup_opts; do
                if [ "$licavail" -eq 1 ]
                then
                        echo $disk >> $pnewerr
                        continue
                fi
                #
                # We save the old value of $disk in $old_disk because $disk
                # will now contain the dmpnode name of that disk. $old_disk
                # needs to be written to $newlist and not $disk.
                #
                old_disk=$disk
                if [ ! -f $mkdbfile ]
                then
        
                # At all places where vxdmpadm is used, if vxdmp module is
                # not installed or if some other error occurs, we use the old
                # value of $disk since in such cases the dmpnode name and value
                # of $disk is going to be the same.

                        dmpout=`/usr/sbin/vxdmpadm getdmpnode \
                                        nodename=${disk} 2>/dev/null | tail +3 \
                                        | cut -d " " -f 1`
                        if [ -n "$dmpout" ]
                        then
                                disk=$dmpout
                        fi
                fi
                dogi_slice_to_device $disk disk
                export disk; ewritemsg -s INFO -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:498 \
                        "Volume Manager: Partitioning $disk as a new disk."
                if not ecmd vxdisksetup -if $disk $setup_opts; then
                        export disk; ewritemsg -s ERROR -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:375 \
                                "The partitioning of $disk failed."
                        echo $disk >> $pnewerr
                else
                        echo $old_disk >> $newlist
                        xcmd touch $newfile
                        xcmd touch $reconfigfile

                fi
        done
        exec 0<&3 3<&-
fi

if [ -f $pcapfile ]; then
        if [ "$licavail" -eq 1 ]
        then
                ewritemsg -s ERROR -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:872 \
                                "No valid license.  Will not encapsulate disks"
        fi
        exec 3<&0 < $pcaplist
        while read disk; do
                if [ "$licavail" -eq 1 ]
                then
                        echo $disk >> $pcaperr
                        continue
                fi
                failed=
                dogi_slice_to_device $disk disk

                # $old_disk is needed by remove_swap() and vxcap-part
                # and also needs to be written to $caplist

                old_disk=$disk
                if [ ! -f $mkdbfile ]
                then
                        dmpout=`/usr/sbin/vxdmpadm getdmpnode \
                                nodename=${disk} 2>/dev/null | \
                                tail +3 | cut -d " " -f 1`
                
                        if [ -n "$dmpout" ]
                        then
                                disk=$dmpout
                        fi
                fi
                dogi_slice_to_device $disk disk
                export disk; ewritemsg -s INFO -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:499 \
                  "Volume Manager: Partitioning $disk as an encapsulated disk."
                if not ecmd remove_swap $old_disk ||
                   not ecmd vxcap-part $old_disk
                then
                        export disk; ewritemsg -s ERROR -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:375 \
                                "The partitioning of $disk failed."
                        echo $disk >> $pcaperr
                else
                        echo $old_disk >> $caplist
                        xcmd touch $capfile
                        xcmd touch $reconfigfile
                fi
        done
        exec 0<&3 3<&-
fi

changes_to_be_undone=0
if [ -s $pnewerr -o -s $pcaperr ]; then
        (
                if [ -s $pnewerr ]; then
                        ewritemsg -s ERROR -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:363 "The following disks failed partitioning:"
                        cat $pnewerr
                fi
                if [ -s $pcaperr ]; then
                        ewritemsg -s ERROR -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:361 "The following disks failed encapsulation:"
                        cat $pcaperr
                fi
        ) | voladm_display
        voladm_continue
        ewritemsg -M vxvmshm:515 \
"You can either continue now, or reverse all changes the Volume Manager
  has made during this reconfiguration."

        if voladm_yorn -M vxvmshm:438 "Undo changes made during partition phase" n; then
                changes_to_be_undone=1
                rm -f $tmpfile1
                if [ -f $pnewlist ]
                then
                        xcmd cat $pnewlist | awk '{print $1}' >> $tmpfile1
                fi
                if [ -f $pcaplist ]
                then
                        xcmd cat $pcaplist >> $tmpfile1
                fi
                exec 3<&0 < $tmpfile1
                while read disk setup_opts; do
                        [ -s $DISKDIR/$disk/vtoc ] || continue
                        old_disk=$disk
                        if [ ! -f $mkdbfile ]
                        then
                                dmpout=`/usr/sbin/vxdmpadm getdmpnode \
                                        nodename=${disk} 2>/dev/null | \
                                        tail +3 | cut -d " " -f 1`
                                if [ -n "$dmpout" ]
                                then
                                        disk=$dmpout
                                fi
                        fi
                        dogi_slice_to_device $disk disk
                        dogi_device_rawpath $disk disk_rawpath

                        primary_node=$disk_rawpath 

                        if [ -f $DISKDIR/$old_disk/primary_node ]       
                            then   
                            exec 3<&0 < $DISKDIR/$old_disk/primary_node
                            read node
                            dogi_slice_to_device $node addr 
                            dogi_device_rawpath $addr primary_node
                        fi  

                        export disk; ewritemsg -s INFO -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:551 "undo $disk...."
                        echo 'y' |
                          $EDVTOC -f $DISKDIR/$old_disk/vtoc $primary_node >/dev/null
                done
                exec 0<&3 3<&-
                rm -f $pnewerr $pcaperr $newlist $caplist  $newfile $capfile
                sync
        fi
fi

rm -f $pcapfile $pcaplist $pnewfile $pnewlist

if [ $reboot = "yes" ]; then
        ewritemsg -s NOTICE -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:392 \
         "The system will now be rebooted to continue the reconfiguration."

        cd /
        sync;sync;uadmin 2 1
fi

# do a vxmend online of all plexes which were offlined as part of the
# upgrade process. At this stage everything should have mounted on volumes

if [ -f $upgrade_reconf ]; then
        sh $upgrade_reconf > /dev/null
        [ $? -eq 0 ] || {
                ugettxt -s NOTICE "
Failed to online some plexes of the volumes created before the upgrade.
You may attempt to online them manually or consult the documentation
for further assistance" vxvmshm:2922
        voladm_continue
        }
        rm -f $upgrade_reconf
fi

if [ $changes_to_be_undone -eq 1 ]; then
        # if any swap areas were removed, add them back
        if [ -n "$swap_removed" ]
        then
                swapadd -1
        fi

        ewritemsg -s NOTICE -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:1337 \
"Changes made during the partition phase were undone..."
        quit 1
fi

if not [ -f $newfile -o -f $capfile ]; then
        # if any swap areas were removed, add them back
        if [ -n "$swap_removed" ]
        then
                swapadd -1
        fi

        quit 0
fi

ewritemsg -s INFO -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:323 \
"The Volume Manager is now reconfiguring (initialization phase)..."
rm -f $newerr $caperr

# # make sure at least 0 length files exist for both, so loops work

[ -f $newlist ] || xcmd touch $newlist
[ -f $caplist ] || xcmd touch $caplist

exec 3<&0 < $newlist
while read disk; do
        old_disk=$disk
        dmpout=`/usr/sbin/vxdmpadm getdmpnode nodename=${disk} 2>/dev/null | \
                        tail +3 | cut -d " " -f 1`
        if [ -n "$dmpout" ]
        then
                disk=$dmpout
        fi
        dgname=`cat $DISKDIR/$old_disk/dg`
        if [ "$dgname" = "$RESERVED_DG_BOOT" ]
        then
                dgname=`vxdg bootdg 2>/dev/null`
        fi
        dogi_slice_to_device $disk disk
        if [ -s $DISKDIR/$old_disk/dmname ]; then
                dmname=`cat $DISKDIR/$old_disk/dmname`
                export dmname disk; ewritemsg -s INFO -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:496 \
                        "Volume Manager: Adding $dmname ($disk) as a new disk."
        else
                dmname=
                export disk; ewritemsg -s INFO -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:494 \
                        "Volume Manager: Adding $disk as a new disk."
        fi
        if not initdisk "$dgname" $disk "$dmname"; then
                echo $disk >> $newerr
                continue;
        fi
done
exec 0<&3 3<&-

exec 3<&0 < $caplist
while read disk; do
        dmpout=`/usr/sbin/vxdmpadm getdmpnode \
                nodename=${disk} 2>/dev/null |  tail +3 | cut -d " " -f 1`
        old_disk=$disk
        if [ -n "$dmpout" ]
        then
                disk=$dmpout
        fi
        dogi_slice_to_device $disk disk
        export disk
        if [ -s $DISKDIR/$old_disk/dmname ]; then
                dmname=`cat $DISKDIR/$old_disk/dmname`
                export dmname disk; ewritemsg -s INFO -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:497 \
        "Volume Manager: Adding $dmname ($disk) as an encapsulated disk."
        else
                dmname=
                export disk; ewritemsg -M vxvmshm:495 \
                        "Volume Manager: Adding $disk as an encapsulated disk."
        fi
        dgname=`cat $DISKDIR/$old_disk/dg`
        if [ "$dgname" = "$RESERVED_DG_BOOT" ]
        then
                dgname=`vxdg bootdg 2>/dev/null`
        fi
        if not remove_swap $old_disk || not initdisk "$dgname" $disk "$dmname"; then
                echo $disk >> $caperr
                continue
        fi
        vxcap-vol $old_disk
        status=$?
        if [ $status -ne 0 -a $status -ne 101 -a $status -ne 102 ]; then
                export disk; ewritemsg -s ERROR -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:329 \
                        "The creation of encapsulated volumes for $disk failed."
                echo $disk >> $caperr
                continue
        fi

        # if vxcap-vol encapsulated the root file system, then we must
        # arrange to start the root file system volume out of the kernel.
        # If we encapsulated a mounted file system then we must reboot.
        if [ $status -eq 102 ]
        then
                if not vxroot $disk; then
                        ewritemsg -s ERROR -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:337 \
                                "The encapsulation of the Boot Disk failed."
                else
                        newroot_path=
                        disksubpath=
                        dogi_node_to_path ${disk}s0 subpath
                        dogi_slice_rawpath $subpath disksubpath
                        prtvtoc -h $disksubpath > $tmpfile1
                        exec 3<&0 < $tmpfile1
                        while read part tag flag; do
                        if [ $part = '*' ]; then
                                continue
                        fi
                        if [ $tag = '2' ]; then
                                slice=$part
                        fi
                        done
                        exec 0<&3 3<&-
                        dogi_device_slice $old_disk $slice newroot_slice
                        dogi_get_prompath $newroot_slice newroot_path
                        if [ -n "$newroot_path" ]
                        then
                                vxeeprom supported && {
                                doit vxeeprom devalias "vx-$dmname" $newroot_path
                        }

                        fi
                fi
                reboot=yes
        elif [ $status -eq 101 ]
        then
                reboot=yes
        fi
done
exec 0<&3 3<&-

rm -f $newfile $capfile $newlist $caplist

if [ -s $newerr -o -s $caperr ]; then
        if [ -s $newerr ]; then
                ewritemsg -s ERROR -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:362 \
                        "The following disks failed initialization:"
                voladm_display $newerr
                voladm_continue
        fi
        if [ -s $caperr ]; then
                ewritemsg -s ERROR -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:361 \
                        "The following disks failed encapsulation:"
                voladm_display $caperr
                voladm_continue
        fi
        rm -f $newerr $caperr
fi

vxdctl bootdg $dgname

if [ $reboot = "yes" ]; then
        sol_rel=`uname -r`
        enclo_name="/vx_lu.$sol_rel/.newnames"
        if [ -f "$enclo_name" ]; then
                cp "$enclo_name" /etc/vx/.newnames
        fi
        ewritemsg -s NOTICE -n vxvm-reconfig -M vxvmshm:393 \
                "The system will now be rebooted."
        cd /
        sync;sync;uadmin 2 1
fi
# if any swap areas were removed, add them back
if [ -n "$swap_removed" ]
then
        swapadd -1
fi
quit 0

/etc/rcS.d/S87vxvm-startvc 

#!/sbin/sh -
# $Id: vxvm-startvc.sh,v 1.2.2.5 2006/03/29 20:38:03 davidl Exp $
#ident "$Source: /project/unixvm-cvs/src/sol/cmd/vxvm/init.d/vxvm-startvc.sh,v $"
#
# $Copyrights: Copyright (c) 2006 Symantec Corporation.
# All rights reserved.
#
# THIS SOFTWARE CONTAINS CONFIDENTIAL INFORMATION AND TRADE SECRETS OF
# SYMANTEC CORPORATION.  USE, DISCLOSURE OR REPRODUCTION IS PROHIBITED
# WITHOUT THE PRIOR EXPRESS WRITTEN PERMISSION OF SYMANTEC CORPORATION.
#
# The Licensed Software and Documentation are deemed to be "commercial
# computer software" and "commercial computer software documentation"
# as defined in FAR Sections 12.212 and DFARS Section 227.7202.  $
#

 ${VOLROOT_DIR:=$__VXVM_ROOT_DIR}
. ${VOL_SCRIPTS_LIB:-$VOLROOT_DIR/usr/lib/vxvm/lib}/vxcommon

PATH=/usr/lib/vxvm/bin:/sbin:/usr/sbin:/usr/bin
progname=vxvm-startvc

#
# Update these variables after they are finalized
#
SANVM_FEATURE_NAME="Client service"
SANVM_NODE_CMD="/etc/vx/diag.d/vxsvmdiag -q maint"
VC_START_OPTS=
VC_START_CMD=startvc

trap "exit 1" INT HUP QUIT TERM

# If volume client is already active, exit silently 
$SANVM_NODE_CMD vcstate
[ $? -eq 1 ] && { exit 0 ; }

# Check for volume client license
vxlictest -n "VERITAS Volume Manager" -f "$SANVM_FEATURE_NAME" > /dev/null 2>&1

[ $? -eq 0 ] && { \
        $SANVM_NODE_CMD $VC_START_OPTS $VC_START_CMD >/dev/null 2>&1
        [ $? -eq 0 ] || { ugettxt -s INFO -n $progname \
                "Volume Client not started" vxvmshm:4529 >&2 ; }
}

exit 0

/etc/rcS.d/S95picld 

#!/sbin/sh
#
# Copyright (c) 1999-2000 by Sun Microsystems, Inc.
# All rights reserved.
#ident   "@(#)picld     1.2     00/06/21 SMI"
#

case "$1" in
'start')
        if [ -x /usr/lib/picl/picld ]; then
                /usr/lib/picl/picld
        fi
        ;;

'stop')
        /usr/bin/pkill -x -u 0 '(picld)'
        ;;

*)
        echo "Usage: $0 { start | stop }"
        exit 1
        ;;
esac
exit 0
